				highlight_color_before_active = 2
			}
	
		available = {
			285 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = CHI is_subject_of = CHI } } }
			517 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = CHI is_subject_of = CHI } } }

			636 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = CHI is_subject_of = CHI } } }
			669 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = CHI is_subject_of = CHI } } }
			674 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = CHI is_subject_of = CHI } } }
			757 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = CHI is_subject_of = CHI } } }
			843 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = CHI is_subject_of = CHI } } }
			985 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = CHI is_subject_of = CHI } } }
			986 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = CHI is_subject_of = CHI } } }
			987 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = CHI is_subject_of = CHI } } }
			988 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = CHI is_subject_of = CHI } } }
		}
	
		fire_only_once = yes
	
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 5
		}
		complete_effect = {
			AST = {
				every_core_state = {
					remove_core_of = AST
				}
			}
			release = AST
			285 = { add_core_of = AST }
			517 = { add_core_of = AST }
			518 = { add_core_of = AST }
			519 = { add_core_of = AST }
			520 = { add_core_of = AST }
			521 = { add_core_of = AST }
			522 = { add_core_of = AST }
			523 = { add_core_of = AST }
			636 = { add_core_of = AST }
			669 = { add_core_of = AST }
			674 = { add_core_of = AST }
			757 = { add_core_of = AST }
			843 = { add_core_of = AST }
			985 = { add_core_of = AST }
			986 = { add_core_of = AST }
			987 = { add_core_of = AST }
			988 = { add_core_of = AST }
	
			AST = { 
				every_core_state = {
				  limit = {
					AND = {
					  NOT = { 
						is_core_of = CHI
					  }
					  OR = {
						is_owned_by = CHI
						OWNER = { is_subject_of = CHI} 
					  }
					}
				  }
				  transfer_state_to = AST
				}
			  }
			AST = { 
				set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_AST_OCC
				load_focus_tree = generic_focus            
	
				set_popularities = {
					syndicalist = 20
					social_democrat = 50
					social_liberal = 5
					market_liberal = 5
					social_conservative = 5
					authoritarian_democrat = 5
					paternal_autocrat = 5
					national_populist = 5
				}
			
				CHI = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = AST
						autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
					}
				}
	
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_democrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
		}
